# `set`-theory model translations — before and after each tactic

Restricted to the **`set`** theory. 342 cases over 6 (task, encoding, scale) groups. Each distinct post-tactic model is shown as an inline diff below its group (self-contained — no smt2 files); sequences yielding an identical model are grouped. Groups ordered fastest-encoding-first; rows within a group by total ms (apply + solve).

## Best translation per group

| task | encoding | N | result | best ms | Δnodes | models |
|---|---|--:|---|--:|--:|--:|
| dispatch | set_bv | 50 | sat | 0.15 | -151 | 18 |
| dispatch | set | 50 | sat | 0.21 | -161 | 26 |
| dispatch | set_bv | 200 | sat | 0.21 | -601 | 18 |
| dispatch | set | 200 | sat | 0.47 | -600 | 26 |
| reachability | unroll_set | 20 | sat | 0.36 | -1606 | 16 |
| reachability | unroll_set | 60 | sat | 41.26 | -25447 | 18 |
